She also accommodated our special needs and assigned us rooms on the highest floor. Also, knowing that it was our anniversary, decorated the rooms beautifully. Also, it was useful to send information on nearby tourist attractions and good restaurants through WeChat. Basically, the service and mindfulness of are excellent.

1. Location: The location of the hotel is really nice. There is an ocean right in front of you, so you can take a walk in the morning and evening. At night, the light shines on the surrounding buildings, so the night view is beautiful. The nearby tourist attraction is not far away, so you can take a taxi in about 10 minutes. 

2. Room Condition: The room is clean as it is a new hotel. I used it well because there was an air purifier. The amenities are sufficiently set up. It is convenient to control the curtains and lights.

3. Breakfast: It was nice to have a meal while looking at the sea at the restaurant, and I could eat Chinese and western styles. The instant noodles and huntun were delicious. It was convenient to make coffee and bring it to me right away.

4. Swimming Pool: I liked the swimming pool the most in this hotel. It was comfortable because I could swim while looking at the sea and there were not many people. 
The people who work in the swimming pool are really nice. I asked them to take a picture because I was alone, and they were willing to take it, so I appreciate it.

If I come to Qingdao again, it is a hotel I want to come back to.üëçüëçüëç

posted:Posted January 11, 2024
msg:Relatively new hotel. Room was spacious and clean, appreciated that it had a bath. Some English spoken by staff, which is increasingly a rarity at even five star hotels in China. Breakfast restaurant had nice views over the ocean and lots of seating, food was decent quality but choice rather limited. The ‚Äúsea view‚Äù room was actually more a view of the tower block opposite, which was disappointing, but you could see the ocean/beach if you stood right by the window. While the hotel is right by the sea, there aren‚Äôt many good restaurants nearby and it‚Äôs a good 20 minute walk to any of the sights (nearest being May 4th Square). Required a large deposit at check-in, despite having paid in advance, and charge for minibar items, which is very old-fashioned approach for a new hotel. Smell of cigarettes in the corridor was unpleasant, so assume some rooms aren‚Äôt non-smoking, which is a shame. The room was very hot, unfortunately the aircon was not very effective at cooling the room down, and noisy, so had to turn it off in the end. The air purifier in the room was appreciated. Lots of free mineral water provided, which was also good, as some hotels only provide 1-2 bottles. Overall, a very good hotel which - with some minor improvements - could be a great one.

From the first day of check-in, Miss Abby was very enthusiastic and added WeChat. She greeted me every day and asked if I wanted to change the spare parts and clean the room. This time, I booked an executive deluxe sea view king room. The bed in the room was very large, and the window faced the third bathing beach. It was great to wake up in the sea view every morning. The bathroom is separated into dry and wet, and the window next to the bathtub is also facing the sea. You can enjoy the scenery while taking a bath. name:l‚Äçe‚Äço‚Äçl‚Äça‚Äçm‚Äçz‚Äçh
info:Executive King Side Sea View
info:Stayed in February 2022
info:Friends
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 28, 2022
msg:Sitting between the mountains and the sea, resting on the clouds.

-design-
The hotel is located in the front row of sea views near Taipingjiao in Qingdao, adjacent to the St. Regis Hotel. As a continuation of the new work of Qingdao Haitian Hotel, the owner of Haitian Hotel also invited CCD to design the interior. The overall style has many design elements from previous works, and also incorporates the local elements of Qingdao. The overall tone is restrained and solemn. In terms of materials, a lot of stone and wood are used, and the cyan color is very prominent in it, but it does not destroy the overall style, which is just right. The use of cyan and green in the executive lounge is more thorough, and the style is also continued.

-Room-
The room size is acceptable, and the semi-open bathroom can make the overall space more open. The independent wardrobe design surrounds the entry and exit positions, the moving lines are reasonable, and it is better in terms of feng shui. The bathroom is only in place, and the washlet is standard. The bathroom accessories used in the executive rooms are Agraria, a San Francisco cleaning and care brand used by InterContinental. The lemon verbena smells very good.
The overall sanitation in the room is quite good, and the bathrobes and slippers are also of the top level. Except for the slightly mediocre selection of the hairdryer, there is nothing wrong with other aspects.
However, among other hardware, the intelligent experience is slightly lower, the intelligence of the room control system is limited, and the basic electric curtains and sunshades are available, but the lighting design is slightly regrettable, the controllable scenes are limited, and the lights at the entrance cannot be turned off directly. A lot of lights in the room are designed in retro gas style. Although they are quite distinctive, they are slightly less practical. Soft wall washers and other surface lights should bring a better experience.
The teapot is a very rare smeg kettle, and the Nespresso and twg tea leaves are also the standard of this level.
The selection of bedding is qualified. The picky point is that there is no fur cushion on the mattress. Fortunately, the softness and support of the mattress are not bad, as well as a variety of optional material pillows, and the sleeping experience is qualified. .
The room is located on the 31st floor of the top floor. The angle of the side sea view is limited by the building next door. The viewing angle is as shown in the figure.

-breakfast-
The breakfast dining environment can be said to be very pleasant. Thanks to the spacious location and reasonable dining flow, the seating guidance and dining experience are very good. The most attractive of course is the invincible sea view. There are also many kinds of breakfast, the ingredients are also very fresh, and the comments from peers are also very good.

-Serve-
The overall service level is online, and the situation is as follows: the executive lounge is located on the 30th floor. Since the tea break time has passed, only soft drinks are available. However, the female staff of the executive lounge saw our 2 rooms. A total of 4 guests in the executive room did not give good guidance after entering, and made an inappropriate reminder when we took the soft drink, and the companion felt a little embarrassed after hearing it. It should be around 20:20 when we entered, the staff has already started cleaning, and they are talking loudly, the experience is slightly poor. In addition, when we checked in and out, the concierge at the entrance of the hotel did not help to take the luggage to the car. I hope the hotel can improve these two points in the future.

-parking-
The location of the parking lot is clear, and the charging pile for the special call is near the entrance of the elevator in the hotel basement, but the equipment is still being debugged until the time of departure. Guests who need charging can check whether it is ready for use in advance.

-grateful-
The space is limited, and the content is based on feelings. In the end, I would like to thank Ge Lingkang, Eric and Nora from the front office, who not only met our needs and helped us arrange the same floor, but also gave a comprehensive introduction to the hotel's facilities and locations. There are also meal times and executive courtesy. I hope colleagues from other depar**ents of the hotel can learn from him about guest service. Next time I come to Qingdao, I will choose to stay at Haitian Hotel.

It is the superior skyline landmark of the city core, leading the new trend of the city. It is the number one luxury hot-selling hotel in Qingdao, with thousands of high praise and excellent reviews online. The lobby of the hotel is large and spacious, and the waterscape of the indoor fountain is peculiar and innovative. The rooms have a natural view, and the panoramic view of Qingdao's sea and mountain views. The rooms are well-equipped, with a small entrance hall, cloakroom, mini bar and so on. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry, with high-end toiletries. Smart access control, smart curtains, smart electric control, smart toilets, etc., are easy to use. When the door is opened, the lights, TV, and curtains are also automatically turned on. Pull open the sanitary door and the toilet lid will open automatically. You can see the sea view when you lie down on the chaise longue. In the executive lounge on the 30th floor of the hotel, you can enjoy the magnificence of the sea and the sky and the invincible city view of red tiles and green trees. The service of the hotel is very good.
